There are a variety of Chinese stir-fries, soups, porridge, noodles and Wuyi Mountain special snacks. It is very suitable for parents. The ecological environment of Wuyi Mountain is very good, and the climbing is not difficult. There is no need for special forces, which is suitable for slow experience. There is also a walking trail behind the hotel, which is also worth walking or jogging. It is very quiet and comfortable.

And my favorite thing is that they gave me 3 room cards directly! One is always plugged into the room for electricity, and two for my wife and I to realize room card freedom!
It should also be noted that there is a housekeeper WeChat here, which is 24-hour service after adding (the shuttle bus is also 24 hours). Because I have to climb Baiyun Zen Temple to watch the sunrise early the next morning after checking in, I need a flashlight. There is a flashlight in the bedside table of each room here!!! Super considerate! And you can apply to borrow more flashlights!! Invincible perfection!!
Then the hotel itself covers a large area, and the internal garden landscape can be visited in about an hour, which is very worth visiting! The design is very good and beautiful. The only regret is that I haven't tried the internal ferry. Haha, every building here is next to the water. You can choose to go by ferry or ferry, which is unique.
There is a gym, swimming pool and spa in the hotel (no time to experience it). Friends who have time and ideas can try it.
The hotel is very convenient for travel. You can either walk to the old street for dinner or go anywhere you want or take a Didi taxi directly. The response speed is fast enough, and the hotel is very well-known here. Any driver knows this hotel.
Finally, let's talk about the room itself. The bed is very comfortable, there is a large bathroom and a large bathtub (I don't have time to experience the bathtub, so I won't comment), and there is a balcony. There are mountains and water outside the balcony. It is really an invincible view. We originally planned to stay in the hotel for a whole day to enjoy this hotel. Although the price has risen near May Day, it is definitely worth the money, absolutely.
I will strongly recommend all my friends to stay in Chunbo, and I will definitely stay again when I come to Wuyi Mountain next time. Thanks to all the hotel staff!

msg:Seeing that the autumn sunshine has been shining brightly these days, I made an impromptu trip to Wuyi Mountain and stayed in my favorite Wuyi Chunbo, making it an easy trip.

In line with the mountains and rivers of Wuyi Mountain, the hotel also integrates the guest rooms into the streams and natural green plants, allowing a green stream to meander in the hotel park.

In the morning light, the park is like a fairy tale world, quiet and graceful, peaceful and peaceful. The rising sunshine gently shines on the trees and flowers, giving the entire park a tranquil artistic conception of "light smoke and flowing water painting a quiet screen" in Qin Guan's poem, with an elegant and graceful style. The color is light and light.

The blue sky, golden trees reflected in the stream, and the protruding Wuyi Mountains in the background are breathtakingly beautiful. The pink beauty's burnt flowers complement the broad green leaves. Through the tall green bamboo forest, you can vaguely see the villa, creating an artistic conception of "thatched cottage with bamboo fence, an isolated village with faint smoke and decaying grass".

Walking in the garden at dusk, a small boat floats leisurely in the stream with flowers and green trees on both sides. I can't help but think of Li Qingzhao's words: "I often remember the sunset in the creek pavilion, and I am so drunk that I don't know the way back. Returning to the boat late after having fun, I stray into the depths of the lotus flowers. Place. Fighting for the crossing, fighting for the crossing, startling a pool of gulls and herons."

When night falls, the bridge in the pool in the central garden lights up. When the pool sprays water mist, there is an ethereal and dreamlike feeling.

Walking out of the side door is the Chongyang Creek Promenade. In October, the sweet-scented osmanthus is in full bloom, and the air is filled with the rich fragrance of sweet-scented osmanthus. The plants along the stream are lush and green, and the roads are clean and tidy. Walking by the stream in the early morning and evening, smelling the fragrance of osmanthus, listening to the chirping of birds, and watching the clear water reflecting the mountain peaks, how pleasant it is!

The breakfast is rich and exquisite, including a variety of Chinese pasta and stir-fry dishes, as well as Western-style cakes and breads. The freshly ground soy milk tastes fresh and rich, and the fillings of Qingming fruit dumplings are delicious.

The room is spacious, the bathroom is particularly large, and you can also take a bath. There is a small yard, and it feels so good to hear the birds chirping in the morning.

The service is truly a five star service that is second to none. When checking in, I casually asked if there was a double bed room. Since I was traveling alone, the hotel immediately put the double beds together to make a double bed. Whenever there is an inquiry, the staff immediately stands up to answer the question with a big smile. The battery car responds to your needs. All employees will greet you politely. All in all, this is an unforgettable hotel.

Finally, the service attitude and quality of the pottery bar are seriously hindering, making people feel like outsourcing.
